Sub UpdateSQLFromCSV()
    Dim conn As Object
    Dim filePath As String
    Dim fileNum As Integer
    Dim lineData As String
    Dim values() As String
    Dim sql As String
    Dim isFirstLine As Boolean
    Dim connStr As String

    ' === CONFIGURE THESE ===
    filePath = "C:\Path\To\Your\File.csv" ' <<<< UPDATE this
    connStr = "Provider=SQLOLEDB;Data Source=YourServer;Initial Catalog=YourDB;Integrated Security=SSPI;" ' <<<< UPDATE this

    ' === Open DB Connection ===
    Set conn = CreateObject("ADODB.Connection")
    conn.Open connStr

    ' === Drop #temp if exists (ignore errors) ===
    On Error Resume Next
    conn.Execute "DROP TABLE #temp"
    On Error GoTo 0

    ' === Create #temp table ===
    sql = "CREATE TABLE #temp (" & _
          "Ref VARCHAR(100), " & _
          "isSACheck BIT, " & _
          "CheckType VARCHAR(50), " & _
          "bulkid INT, " & _
          "lastupdatedby VARCHAR(50), " & _
          "lastupdateddate DATETIME, " & _
          "ITsToolId INT)"
    conn.Execute sql

    ' === Open and Read CSV File ===
    fileNum = FreeFile
    Open filePath For Input As #fileNum

    isFirstLine = True

    Do While Not EOF(fileNum)
        Line Input #fileNum, lineData

        ' Skip header row
        If isFirstLine Then
            isFirstLine = False
            Continue Do
        End If

        values = Split(lineData, ",")

        ' Assumes CSV has 7 columns: Ref, isSACheck, CheckType, bulkid, lastupdatedby, lastupdateddate, ITsToolId
        If UBound(values) >= 6 Then
            sql = "INSERT INTO #temp (Ref, isSACheck, CheckType, bulkid, lastupdatedby, lastupdateddate, ITsToolId) VALUES (" & _
                  "'" & Replace(Trim(values(0)), "'", "''") & "', " & _
                  IIf(Trim(values(1)) = "1" Or LCase(Trim(values(1))) = "true", 1, 0) & ", " & _
                  "'" & Replace(Trim(values(2)), "'", "''") & "', " & _
                  Val(Trim(values(3))) & ", " & _
                  "'" & Replace(Trim(values(4)), "'", "''") & "', " & _
                  "'" & Format(CDate(Trim(values(5))), "yyyy-mm-dd hh:nn:ss") & "', " & _
                  Val(Trim(values(6))) & ")"

            conn.Execute sql
        End If
    Loop

    Close #fileNum

    ' === Update Main SQL Table ===
    sql = "UPDATE tgt SET " & _
          "tgt.isSACheck = tmp.isSACheck, " & _
          "tgt.CheckType = tmp.CheckType, " & _
          "tgt.bulkid = tmp.bulkid, " & _
          "tgt.lastupdatedby = tmp.lastupdatedby, " & _
          "tgt.lastupdateddate = tmp.lastupdateddate, " & _
          "tgt.ITsToolId = tmp.ITsToolId " & _
          "FROM YourTargetTable tgt INNER JOIN #temp tmp ON tgt.Ref = tmp.Ref"
    conn.Execute sql

    ' === Clean up ===
    conn.Close
    Set conn = Nothing

    MsgBox "Update complete."

End Sub



Private Sub Command0_Click()
 Dim filePath As String
    Dim fileNum As Integer
    Dim LineOfText As String
    Dim RecordCount As Long

    Dim line As String
    Dim fields() As String
  

    filePath = "C:\TKEDoc\TempWork\DataImport.csv" ' Change to your actual file path
    fileNum = FreeFile
    
    
    
    On Error GoTo ErrHandler
        
    Open filePath For Input As #fileNum
    
    RecordCount = 0
    
    ' Skip header row if present
    Line Input #fileNum, LineOfText ' Uncomment this line if your CSV has headers
    
    Do While Not EOF(fileNum)
        Line Input #fileNum, LineOfText
        fields = Split(LineOfText, ",")
        Debug.Print fields(0), fields(1), fields(2)
        If Trim(LineOfText) <> "" Then
            RecordCount = RecordCount + 1
        End If
    Loop
    
    Close #fileNum
    
    MsgBox "Total number of records: " & RecordCount

    Exit Sub

ErrHandler:
    MsgBox "Error reading file: " & Err.Description
    If fileNum > 0 Then Close #fileNum

End Sub

SELECT DISTINCT a.SrcCDCustomerID, a.DateTaken
FROM SRG_SrcCDDebt a
JOIN SRG_SrcCDCustomer cust_148 ON a.SrcCDCustomerID = cust_148.SrcCDCustomerID
JOIN SRG_SrcCDCustomer cust_149 
    ON cust_148.CustomerID = cust_149.CustomerID
    AND cust_148.AdviceID = cust_149.AdviceID
    AND cust_148.SRCMasterID = 148
    AND cust_149.SRCMasterID = 149
WHERE a.SRCMasterID = 148;


----------------

SELECT COALESCE (pr.TopUpID, pr.RBS_Policy_Number, pr.UPID) AS TopUpID,cg.AdviceID,cg.ContactGroupID, pc.FROutcome, 
pc.QCOutcome,qc.QcRAGRef,qc.SRCMasterID,qc.InitialLoadDate,qc.QCNameID,qc.QCTeamLeaderID,qc.DateQCCheckStarted, 
qc.QCCheckType,qc.QCOverallGrade,qc.QcRAGVersion, qc.reworkrequired,qc.reworksummary ,
cgq.Grading,cgq.Comments FROM SRG_ProductCustomerGrouping p 
Left Join SRC_QC_CaseLevel qc on p.CaseID = qc.CaseID 
Left Join SRC_QC_ContactGroup cg on qc.QCCaseID = cg.QCCaseID 
Left join SRG_Product pr on p.ProductID=pr.ProductID 
Left Join SRC_QC_ProductOutcomes pc on cg.QCContGroupID = pc.QCContGroupID 
Left Join SRC_QC_ContactGroupQuestions cgq on cgq.QCContGroupID=pc.QCContGroupID 
Where P.CaseID = 75607 AND  qc.QCCaseID = '123'


--------------------

WITH cgq_deduped AS (
  SELECT *, 
         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY QCContGroupID ORDER BY Grading DESC) AS rn
  FROM SRC_QC_ContactGroupQuestions
)

SELECT ...
FROM SRG_ProductCustomerGrouping p
LEFT JOIN SRC_QC_CaseLevel qc ON p.CaseID = qc.CaseID
LEFT JOIN SRC_QC_ContactGroup cg ON qc.QCCaseID = cg.QCCaseID
LEFT JOIN SRG_Product pr ON p.ProductID = pr.ProductID
LEFT JOIN SRC_QC_ProductOutcomes pc ON cg.QCContGroupID = pc.QCContGroupID
LEFT JOIN cgq_deduped cgq ON cgq.QCContGroupID = pc.QCContGroupID AND cgq.rn = 1
WHERE p.CaseID = 75607 AND qc.QCCaseID = '123'
Option 2: Aggregate cgq before joining
If
